[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA medium-severity Server-Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m issue was detected when [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing a ZIP archive under fuzz testing. The fuzzer-triggered code path [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempted an outbound HTTP connection to “jazze.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m[39m,” causing the Jazzer SSRF [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitizer to raise a `FuzzerSecurityIssueMedium`. This indicates that untrusted [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata in the archive can drive network requests, potentially exposing internal [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mservices or leaking sensitive information.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Overview  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During fuzzing of ZIP archive processing [0m[1;39m([0m[39min [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`CompressZipFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the code invoked [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mjava.net.URL.openStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, which in turn used `HttpURLConnection` to connect to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39man external host. The Jazzer SSRF sanitizer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ServerSideRequestForgery.checkSsrf`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintercepted this attempt and reported a medium-severity security issue.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The issue is classified as Server-Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. SSRF [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerabilities arise when attacker-controlled data influences network requests, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallowing access to internal or protected services, or exfiltration of data.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The exception stack trace shows the SSRF check in [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ServerSideRequestForgery.checkSsrf` and `checkSsrfSocket`, indicating jazzer’s [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mruntime protection caught the outbound connection.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The outbound request originated from ZIP file parsing code in Apache Commons [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCompress [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ZipFile.readCentralDirectoryEntry` → `populateFromCentralDirectory` → [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`new ZipFile` constructors[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`CompressZipFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m feeds arbitrary [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata into `new [0m[1;35mZipFile[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, which may contain crafted entries that trigger HTTP [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconnections.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The destination host [0m[1;39m([0m[39m“jazze.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m[39m”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and port were derived from untrusted [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput, confirming the SSRF scenario.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Areas for Investigation  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. **Fuzzer Harness**: `CompressZipFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput` to understand how [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput bytes are passed to the ZIP processing logic.  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. **ZIP Parsing Logic**: Apache Commons Compress classes, specifically [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ZipFile.readCentralDirectoryEntry` and related constructors, to see how URL [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreferences in ZIP entries are handled.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. **Network Request Path**: Java’s `HttpURLConnection` stack [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`openStream`, `plainConnect`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to trace how external hosts are resolved and [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconnected.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. **SSRF Sanitizer**: [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.ServerSideRequestForgery` to review the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdetection mechanism and the criteria for flagging.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. **Input Handling**: Any code that reads or interprets URI/URL content embedded[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min ZIP entries or other archive metadata.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis holistic view will help assess how untrusted archive contents can lead to SSRF[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand what parts of the codebase are involved in request construction and execution.[0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The SSRF vulnerability stems from ZipFile.readCentralDirectoryEntry [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1550[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m1556[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, where any ZIP entry comment beginning with [0m[32m"http"[0m[39m or [0m[32m"https"[0m[39m is treated[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mas a remote URL and fetched unconditionally via `new [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mURL[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcommentString[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.openStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. Since `commentString` is directly derived from [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted archive data, a malicious ZIP can force outbound [0m[1;35mHTTP[0m[1;39m([0m[39mS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m connections.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preservation of Critical Logic[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The only feature impacted by this change is the automatic fetching of remote [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontent in ZIP entry comments. All other ZIP processing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mentry name handling, file [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction, CRC checks, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains unchanged.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No existing public APIs are removed. The `[0m[1;35mZipArchiveEntry.getComment[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrelated methods still return the comment string, albeit without remote fetching [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mside effects.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Proposed Mitigation[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Disable automatic URL fetch by default:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Remove the code block performing `new [0m[1;35mURL[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcommentString[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.openStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Always treat comments starting with [0m[32m"http"[0m[35m/[0m[32m"https"[0m[39m as literal comment text.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOptionally[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Preserve the ability to fetch remote comment content behind an [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexplicit opt-in:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Introduce a new static flag or system property, e.g.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          `org.apache.commons.compress.zip.allowCommentUrlFetch` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdefault: [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`false`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Guard the URL-fetching block with this flag. Only when set to `true` will [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode fetch remote content.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Provide public API methods or Javadoc to guide users on how to enable this [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior if genuinely needed.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Update Javadoc and release notes:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Document that automatic comment URL resolution is disabled by default in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis release.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Explain how users can opt in if they relied on that behavior.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Detailed Steps to Implement[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Open `src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/zip/ZipFile.java`.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Locate the block:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mcommentString.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;35mcommentString.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"https"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = new [0m[1;35mURL[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcommentString[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.openStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[33m...[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIOException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m[39m [0m[1;39m}[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Remove or comment out this entire `if` block so that `commentString` remains [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged after `[0m[1;35mentryEncoding.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcomment[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOptional[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Before removal, insert:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m NEW CONFIG FLAG: disable automatic URL fetch by default[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        private static final boolean ALLOW_COMMENT_URL_FETCH =[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mBoolean.getBoolean[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"org.apache.commons.compress.zip.allowCommentUrlFetc[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mh"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Then replace the unconditional `if` check with:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mALLOW_COMMENT_URL_FETCH && [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mcommentString.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http"[0m[1;39m)[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            || [0m[1;35mcommentString.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"https"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m[39m [0m[1;39m}[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Ensure no other code paths trigger outbound URL connections based on ZIP [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry data.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Add Javadoc above the new flag [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor in class-level comments[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m explaining [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefault behavior and opt-in mechanism.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m. Run the full test suite to confirm no regressions. Existing tests for comment[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandling should still pass, since they do not expect external HTTP calls.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By removing the unconditional URL fetch, we completely eliminate the SSRF [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvector arising from untrusted ZIP comments.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The change is localized to a single method [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`readCentralDirectoryEntry`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdoes not affect other archive formats or utility functions.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Introducing an explicit opt-in preserves backward compatibility for rare users[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwho intentionally rely on remote comment resolution.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach avoids broad exception-catching or reliance on external [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibraries, adhering to best practices without modifying harness or test code.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigation[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Users who previously embedded URLs in comments to pull in remote metadata will[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlose that behavior unless they set the new system property.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mitigation: Clearly document the opt-in flag in release notes and migration [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mguides.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No impact on ZIP file extraction, compression ratios, or other archive [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfeatures.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. References to Similar Patterns[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Many libraries disable automatic network protocols in metadata parsing by [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefault. For example, XML parsers disable DTD fetching unless explicitly [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfigured. Our solution parallels that safe-by-default approach.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m. No Further Code Retrieval Needed  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All necessary context for this fix resides within [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ZipFile.readCentralDirectoryEntry`. No changes to harness code, tests, or external[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodules are required.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m public class ZipFile implements Closeable [0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn SSRF finding was raised by Jazzer when the ZIP‐file handling code in [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ZipFile.java` attempted to open a URL from an entry’s comment. To mitigate [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munrestricted comment-based URL fetching, a patch was proposed that adds a JVM flag [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`org.apache.commons.compress.zip.allowCommentUrlFetch`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and wraps the remote-URL [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic in an `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mALLOW_COMMENT_URL_FETCH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` guard. Applying this patch resulted in [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdozens of compiler errors—mostly “illegal start of type” and “\<identifier\> [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpected”—indicating the patch was inserted at an invalid location or with [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalformed syntax, causing the build to fail.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - During fuzz testing with Jazzer, a `FuzzerSecurityIssueMedium: Server Side [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRequest Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` exception was thrown.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The stack trace showed that `ServerSideRequestForgery.checkSsrfSocket` [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintercepted a connection attempt to `jazze.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m[39m` originating from `new [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mURL[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcommentString[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.openStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.zip.ZipFile.readCentralDirectoryEntry`.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer’s crashing input was a crafted ZIP file whose entry comment began [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith “http…”, triggering a remote-fetch in `ZipFile` and flagged as an SSRF.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The patch adds at the top of `ZipFile.java`:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • A new class header [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`public class ZipFile implements Archive, [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCloseableResource`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • A static boolean `ALLOW_COMMENT_URL_FETCH` controlled by a system property  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It then modifies the existing comment-URL block so that remote fetch only [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moccurs if `ALLOW_COMMENT_URL_FETCH` is true:[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```diff[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mcommentString.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;35mcommentString.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"https"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     + if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mALLOW_COMMENT_URL_FETCH[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     +     && [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mcommentString.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http"[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     +         || [0m[1;35mcommentString.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"https"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = new [0m[1;35mURL[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcommentString[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.openStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[33m...[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The intention is to disable URL fetching by default for security, allowing [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mopt-in via `-Dorg.apache.commons.compress.zip.[0m[33mallowCommentUrlFetch[0m[39m=[0m[35mtrue[0m[39m`.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Result & Observations  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The build failed with roughly [0m[1;36m57[0m[39m errors, all of the form:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • “illegal start of type”  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • “\<identifier\> expected”  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • “reached end of file while parsing”  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The first errors point at line [0m[1;36m51[0m[39m, column [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m in `ZipFile.java`, where the new [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`public class ZipFile` declaration was inserted.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The errors strongly suggest that the patch was placed inside an existing class[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor between imports, breaking the file’s overall structure [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., a nested class [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeclaration outside of any scope or missing closing braces[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Areas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The top of `ZipFile.java` around existing package and import statements: [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mverify the correct position to insert new fields and flags without disrupting the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclass declaration.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The original class signature and implemented interfaces in `ZipFile.java`: [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensure patch does not duplicate or incorrectly redefine the class.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Matching braces and file termination: confirm that no `[0m[1;39m{[0m[39m` or `[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` was [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maccidentally dropped or added, leading to “reached end of file while parsing.”  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The import block ordering: make sure that new imports [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif any[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are placed [0m     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1737[0m[39m:     *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1738[0m[39m:    public IOStream<? extends ZipArchiveEntry> [0m[1;35mstream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1739[0m[39m:        return [0m[1;35mIOStream.adapt[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mentries.stream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1740[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1741[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Revert Incorrect Class Header Insertion[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The last patch attempt erroneously inserted a second `public class ZipFile [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplements Archive, CloseableResource [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` at the top of `ZipFile.java`, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdisrupting imports and the file structure.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove all lines added around the imports [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m39[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m47[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that redefine the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclass and its interfaces. Restore the original `public class ZipFile implements [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCloseable [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m` declaration at line [0m[1;36m95[0m[39m with no duplicates elsewhere.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Add a Static Flag in the Existing Class Scope[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Locate the primary class header in `ZipFile.java`:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     public class ZipFile implements Closeable [0m[1;39m{[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Immediately below this line [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbefore any nested types or methods[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, insert two [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnew static fields:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          * JVM property to opt in to comment‐based URL fetching in ZIP entries.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          * Default is false, disabling remote fetch to prevent SSRF.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          * Enable with -Dorg.apache.commons.compress.zip.[0m[33mallowCommentUrlFetch[0m[39m=[0m[35mtrue[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         private static final String ALLOW_COMMENT_URL_FETCH_PROPERTY =[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[32m"org.apache.commons.compress.zip.allowCommentUrlFetch"[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         private static final boolean ALLOW_COMMENT_URL_FETCH =[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mBoolean.getBoolean[0m[1;39m([0m[39mALLOW_COMMENT_URL_FETCH_PROPERTY[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No additional imports are required since `Boolean.getBoolean` and `String` are[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpart of `java.lang`.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Guard the Remote‐Fetch Logic with the New Flag[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In the `readCentralDirectoryEntry` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround the comment‐fetch block at [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlines ~[0m[1;36m1550[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m1556[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, change the existing unconditional check:[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mcommentString.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;35mcommentString.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"https"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     to a guarded check:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mALLOW_COMMENT_URL_FETCH[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             && [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mcommentString.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcommentString.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"https"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This ensures that remote URL opening [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`new [0m[1;35mURL[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcommentString[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.openStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39monly occurs when the JVM property is explicitly set to true. By default, comments [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeginning with “http”[0m[35m/[0m[39m“https” are treated as literal text and do not trigger [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnetwork requests.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preserve Brace Balance and Class Structure[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Since the only added braces belong to the new `if` guard [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmatching the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moriginal `try` block[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and all new fields are declared inside the existing class [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbody, no braces are lost or orphaned. This resolves the “reached end of file while [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing” and “illegal start of type” compilation errors.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Maintain Existing Functionality and Test Compatibility[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By default, URL‐based comment fetching remains disabled, preventing SSRF [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring fuzzing or other automated tests.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Downstream code that relies on comment‐based fetch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif any[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m can re‐enable it [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msafely via the documented JVM property; existing tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich should not rely on [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal network calls[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continue to pass unchanged.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJustification:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Restores the original class declaration and import block, eliminating malformed [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msyntax.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Introduces a minimal, self‐contained feature flag to control SSRF‐vulnerable code[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpaths, following the original security proposal.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
